msg:It was my first time in Yangzhou and I had a great experience! This is thanks to our choice of Yangzhou Xiyuan Hotel. At first, it was because this hotel seemed to be convenient to various attractions. When we arrived at the hotel, we found many advantages and advantages. Geographical location: Caihong Bridge is at the door, and we had tea at Yechun Tea House. We also had dinner there, which was very good. Geyuan and Guandong Street are just a short walk away. Slender West Lake and Zhu Ziqing's former residence are very convenient.
Hotel decoration (one of the earliest hotels in Yangzhou): The lobby is quite standard, and you can still feel the solemnity and dignity of the year. The service attitude is sincere. There is a younger gentleman at the door, and his service makes you feel at home. Very good!
We upgraded to an executive room. The room is large, the decoration is quite standard, and there is a large cloakroom, which is very convenient. The sofa is too old and dirty. Everything else is very good. The bathroom is large and clean, and the overall lighting is not bad.
The breakfast is really average, but the yogurt is super delicious. I recommend you to try it.

After all, in areas where people don't have to worry about food, clothing and shelter, the promotion and dissemination of culture is also one of the magic weapons for the long-term prosperity of enterprises. The small lacquerware gift given by the front desk when checking out is a manifestation of cultural connotation.

Get off the car, there is a handsome brother to help with luggage, guide check-in. Arrived late, the front desk helped upgrade the suite, spacious, warm and elegant, with the feeling of an old movie. The details are true, the environment and sanitation are impeccable, and the details are caring. There are instructions for use of the coffee machine. There is a small cloakroom and a dressing mirror at the entrance. There is a rotary button on the wall that can play soft music. Beautiful tea sets, beautiful ceramic aromatherapy, ink paintings hanging on the wall, the wall is wrapped with gray leather wainscoting, and there is a marble platform in front of the floor-to-ceiling window. Entering the bedroom, soft disposable slippers have been neatly placed under the stool in front of the bed. There are two bathrooms, a guest bathroom outside and a master bathroom inside. The master bathroom has a bathtub and double sinks, and the walls are warm marble and shell patterns, which are pleasing to the eye and high-end. A spare roll of toilet paper is packed in a beautiful cloth bag. The shower has plenty of water, the environment is quiet, and I had a good night's sleep. If I come to Yangzhou next time, I will choose Xiyuan Hotel again. It will feel like home!
